Quiklrn aggregates all the highlights at a single place for the entire book; these are listed together on the right swipe for the page and entire book in the form of notes.\r\nSo you don’t need to go through the entire book to see the highlights that you made.\r\n\r\nRead aloud\r\nSelecting any text in the reader view opens up more options on the bottom bar. Simply tap the Read Aloud button to listen to the selected text. You can also listen to the whole page by clicking the Read Aloud button in the bottom toggle bar\r\n\r\nQref\r\nQuiklrn has a built-in recommendation engine that suggests additional references, for an improved learning experience.
